0                                  33647              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                   33648              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   33649              Ÿ        The Special Character processing table is defined            Ÿ
                                   33650              Ÿ          with the FCHAR macro.  The format is:                      Ÿ
                                   33651              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   33652              Ÿ              FCHAR  sequence,                                       Ÿ
                                   33653              Ÿ                       TEXT='plain text string to use',              Ÿ
                                   33654              Ÿ                       ALT='x'   "x" is the character in the         Ÿ
                                   33655              Ÿ                                 (Samson) alternate character        Ÿ
                                   33656              Ÿ                                 set.                                Ÿ
                                   33657              Ÿ                       CASE={ANY|UPPER|LOWER}                        Ÿ
                                   33658              Ÿ                                 Specifies that the sequence         Ÿ
                                   33659              Ÿ                                 must be in upper, lower or          Ÿ
                                   33660              Ÿ                                 any case.                           Ÿ
                                   33661              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
0                                  33662                       MACRO
                                   33663              &L       FCHAR &CHARS,&RTN=0,&TEXT=,&ALT=,&CASE=ANY
                                   33664                       GBLA  &FCHARCNT
                                   33665                       GBLC  &FCHARLAB
                                   33666              &L       DS    0F
                                   33667
                                   33668                       AIF   ('&CHARS' EQ '').ENDTAB
                                   33669              .*
                                   33670              &FCHARLAB LABEL
                                   33671              &CHLAB   SETC  '$$$FCHAR&FCHARCNT'
                                   33672              .*
                                   33673              &FCHARCNT SETA &FCHARCNT+1
                                   33674              &FCHARLAB SETC '$$$FCHAR&FCHARCNT'
                                   33675              .*
                                   33676                       DC    A(&FCHARLAB)        Next FCHAR entry ptr
                                   33677              .*
                                   33678                       DC    AL1(L'FCHARF&CASE)  Case flag
                                   33679              .*
                                   33680                       AIF   ('&ALT' EQ '').ALTNONE
                                   33681                       DC    AL1(C&ALT)          Alternate character
                                   33682                       AGO   .ALTCOM
                                   33683              .ALTNONE DC    AL1(0)              No alternate character
                                   33684              .ALTCOM  ANOP
                                   33685              .*
                                   33686                       DC    AL2(0)              Reserved
                                   33687              .*
                                   33688                       DC    A(&RTN)             Processing routine addr
                                   33689              .*
                                   33690                       DC    AL1(L'&CHLAB.C)
                                   33691              &CHLAB.C DC    C&CHARS             Character string user types
                                   33692                       AIF   ('&TEXT' NE '').GOTTEXT
                                   33693                       DC    AL1(0)              No text we can display
                                   33694                       AGO   .TEXTCOM
                                   33695              .GOTTEXT ANOP
                                   33696                       DC    AL1(L'&CHLAB.T)
                                   33697              &CHLAB.T DC    C&TEXT              Character string we display
                                   33698              .TEXTCOM ANOP
